        <h1 class="Article__Title-ejf3ys-0 kUhord"><a href="/blog/2021/06/04/this-week-in-matrix-2021-06-04">This Week in Matrix 2021-06-04</a></h1>
        <div class="Subline-z3aujq-0 fCCPho">
         2021-06-04<!-- --> —&nbsp;<a href="/blog/category/this-week-in-matrix">This Week in Matrix</a> —&nbsp;<!-- -->Ben Parsons
        </div>
        <div class="Article__PostContent-ejf3ys-1 dltekG">
         <h2 id="matrix-live-" style="position:relative"><a href="#matrix-live-" aria-label="matrix live  permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Matrix Live ?</h2>
         <div class="gatsby-resp-iframe-wrapper" style="padding-bottom:56.25%;position:relative;height:0;overflow:hidden"> <iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Dsr6h-0lwWU" title="YouTube video player" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen style="position:absolute;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%"></iframe> 
         </div>
         <h2 id="dept-of-status-of-matrix-?" style="position:relative"><a href="#dept-of-status-of-matrix-%EF%B8%8F" aria-label="dept of status of matrix ? permalink" class="anchor before">

            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Dept of <em>Status of Matrix</em> ??</h2>
         <h3 id="wired-uk-feature-article" style="position:relative"><a href="#wired-uk-feature-article" aria-label="wired uk feature article permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Wired UK feature article</h3>
         <p>Wired UK have published a feature on Matrix in their print edition this month. We'll be sure to link to it when it's made available online!</p>
         <p><img src="/blog/img/2021-06-04-wired.png" alt="Wired Article"></p>
         <h3 id="german-universities-poll" style="position:relative"><a href="#german-universities-poll" aria-label="german universities poll permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>German-universities poll</h3>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@jfkimmes:matrix.org" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">jfkimmes</a> shared:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>I just learned that in a poll of 89 universities in Germany, Matrix ranked third place in the chat category already. </p>
          <p>The source is in only available in German, unfortunately: <a href="https://zenodo.org/record/4817795" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">https://zenodo.org/record/4817795</a></p>
          <p>However, the conclusion list (first table) may be understandable from context. It lists the top three solutions per category with their respective number of universities using it.</p>
         </blockquote>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@oleg:fiksel.info" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Oleg</a> clarified:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>The evaluation was "which solution are you using".</p>
         </blockquote>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@florian:dsn.tm.kit.edu" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Florian</a> added:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>The Instant Messaging part starts at slide 15, the first chart on that slide is "which solution do you use", the second is "How content are you with the solution?", with Matrix having the best average of all solutions, namely ~8.8/10.</p>
         </blockquote>
         <p>also <a href="https://matrix.to/#/@jan.christian:gruenhage.xyz" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">JCG</a>:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>What's also noteworthy: Those using matrix are the happiest with the solution</p>
         </blockquote>
         <p>\o/</p>
         <h2 id="dept-of-spec-" style="position:relative"><a href="#dept-of-spec-" aria-label="dept of spec  permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Dept of Spec ?</h2>
         <h3 id="spec" style="position:relative"><a href="#spec" aria-label="spec permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Spec</h3>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@andrewm:amorgan.xyz" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">anoa</a> offered:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>Here's your weekly spec update! The heart of Matrix is the specification - and this is modified by Matrix Spec Change (MSC) proposals. Learn more about how the process works at <a href="https://spec.matrix.org/unstable/proposals" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">https://spec.matrix.org/unstable/proposals</a>.</p>
          <h4 id="msc-status" style="position:relative"><a href="#msc-status" aria-label="msc status permalink" class="anchor before">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
             <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
            </svg></a>MSC Status</h4>
          <p><strong>New MSCs:</strong></p>
          <ul>
           <li><p><a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/matrix-doc/pull/3231" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">MSC3231: Token authenticated registration</a></p></li>
           <li><p><a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/matrix-doc/pull/3230" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">MSC3230: Spaces top level order</a></p></li>
           <li><p><a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/matrix-doc/pull/3226" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">MSC3226: Per-room spell check</a></p></li>
          </ul>
          <p><strong>MSCs with proposed Final Comment Period:</strong></p>
          <ul>
           <li><em>No MSCs entered proposed FCP state this week.</em></li>
          </ul>
          <p><strong>MSCs in Final Comment Period:</strong></p>
          <ul>
           <li><em>No MSCs are in FCP.</em></li>
          </ul>
          <p><strong>Merged MSCs:</strong></p>
          <ul>
           <li><em>No MSCs were merged this week.</em></li>
          </ul>
          <h4 id="spec-updates" style="position:relative"><a href="#spec-updates" aria-label="spec updates permalink" class="anchor before">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
             <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
            </svg></a>Spec Updates</h4>
          <p>This week the Spec Core Team has been reviewing various Spaces MSCs, most recently <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/matrix-doc/pull/3230" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">MSC3230</a> (Space ordering). We're also hoping to square away the <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/matrix-doc/pull/1849#issuecomment-655153491" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">aggregations MSCs</a> (message editing, reactions, etc) once and for all, though this will likely take a concerted effort from a few members to pull off.</p>
          <p>Finally <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/matrix-doc/pull/3231" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">MSC3231</a> is a (currently draft status) MSC from Callum, one of Matrix.org's <a href="https://matrix.org/blog/2021/05/20/google-summer-of-code-2021" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">GSoC students</a> this year! His project aims to allow native token-based registration to homeservers (the idea is so that you can generate a few tokens from your registration-disabled homeserver and hand them out to a few trusted friends and family members).</p>
          <p>And finally, work still continues on finishing up the technical portions of the new release process for the spec. As mentioned last week, we've attempted to split the work up over multiple people in order to get it done quicker. Slowly but surely...</p>
         </blockquote>
         <p><img src="/blog/img/2021-06-04-I-r8I-stacked_area_chart.png" alt="2021-06-04-I-r8I-stacked_area_chart.png"></p>
         <h2 id="dept-of-servers-" style="position:relative"><a href="#dept-of-servers-" aria-label="dept of servers  permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Dept of Servers ?</h2>
         <h3 id="synapse" style="position:relative"><a href="#synapse" aria-label="synapse permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Synapse</h3>
         <p>Synapse is a popular homeserver written in Python.</p>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@callahad:matrix.org" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">callahad</a> said:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>Hello from the Synapse team! A short update for a short workweek (thanks, bank holidays!):</p>
          <ul>
           <li><p>Synapse 1.35 <a href="https://matrix.org/blog/2021/06/01/synapse-1-35-0-released" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">was released</a> this week! The Spaces flag is on by default, a bunch of bugs were fixed, and we've landed many of the prerequisites to eliminating RAM spikes on room joins.</p></li>
           <li><p>? We have new docs! ? Anoa converted our docs to build with mdbook (<a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/pull/10086" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#10086</a>), and you can now browse them at <a href="https://matrix-org.github.io/synapse/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">https://matrix-org.github.io/synapse/</a>! Check it out and let us know what you think. (Note: Not all of the pages have been converted from reStructuredText to Markdown yet, so some might render a bit strangely, but the structure is there!)</p></li>
          </ul>
          <p>Catch you next Friday! ?</p>
         </blockquote>
         <p><img src="/blog/img/2021-06-04-bILM1-image.png" alt="2021-06-04-bILM1-image.png"></p>
         <h3 id="synapse-media-proxy" style="position:relative"><a href="#synapse-media-proxy" aria-label="synapse media proxy permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">

         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@f0x:pixie.town" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">f0x</a> announced:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>Another round of updates on my smart caching media proxy. After refactoring a lot (as always), I implemented <strong>thumbnailing</strong>! Now the only big feature left to add is url previewing. I also have a test deployment configured on media.pixie.town now, so you can try fetching a bit of remote media through there, or view <a href="https://media.pixie.town/_matrix/media/r0/download/media.pixie.town/GLhyjFL8MPAzz5Oh1gIzF3lQ" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">this submissions screenshot</a></p>

            </svg></a>metrics</h4>
          <p>Got started implementing a Prometeus /metrics endpoint, with a <a href="https://stats.pixie.town/d/rPBvoh6Gk/synapse-media-proxy?orgId=1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">rudimentary Grafana dashboard</a> for my test installation. </p>
          <h4 id="comparison-with-matrix-media-repo" style="position:relative"><a href="#comparison-with-matrix-media-repo" aria-label="comparison with matrix media repo permalink" class="anchor before">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
             <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
            </svg></a>comparison with <a href="https://github.com/turt2live/matrix-media-repo/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">matrix-media-repo</a></h4>
          <p>While they both implement Matrix' media endpoints, they serve rather different niches, where matrix-media-repo fully decouples the media repo aspect, my proxy cooperates with Synapse's filesystem and database, to speed up operation while ultimately making it a seamless drop-in and removal process.</p>
          <p><a href="https://media.pixie.town/_matrix/media/r0/download/im_a/teapot" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">also</a> :P</p>
         </blockquote>

           </svg></a>Security release for the matrix-appservice-irc and matrix-appservice-bridge library</h3>
         <blockquote>
          <p>Hello. This week we've released an update to the <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/matrix-appservice-bridge/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">https://github.com/matrix-org/matrix-appservice-bridge/</a> library containing a security fix for room upgrade handling. The security report will come later, but for now we advise anyone using the room upgrade handler feature to upgrade to <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/matrix-appservice-bridge/releases/tag/2.6.1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">2.6.1</a>. By the same token, we would also advise <em>all</em> IRC bridge admins to update their bridge to <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/matrix-appservice-irc/releases/tag/0.26.1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">0.26.1</a>.</p>
         </blockquote>

         <h3 id="matrix-puppeteer-line" style="position:relative"><a href="#matrix-puppeteer-line" aria-label="matrix puppeteer line permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>matrix-puppeteer-line</h3>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@fair:miscworks.net" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Fair</a> reported:</p>
         <p><a href="https://src.miscworks.net/fair/matrix-puppeteer-line" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">matrix-puppeteer-line</a>: A bridge for LINE Messenger based on running LINE's Chrome extension in Puppeteer.</p>
         <blockquote>
          <ul>
           <li>Send a bridge notice when getting unexpectedly logged out of LINE, to warn you to log in again.</li>
           <li>Improve resiliency of LINE user avatar syncing.</li>
           <li>Properly support syncing LINE rooms with participants who aren't in your LINE friends list (This was harder than it sounds...!)</li>
          </ul>
          <p>These changes (and ones before it) will be merged to <code class="language-text">master</code> once I reorganize some messy commits.</p>
          <p>The next big task is still to fix outbound read receipts (i.e. to make it so that the bridge syncing a message doesn't make your &gt; LINE contacts think you actually read that message). Once that is done, I'll consider the bridge to be in beta.</p>
          <p>Discussion: <a href="https://matrix.to/#/#matrix-puppeteer-line:miscworks.net" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#matrix-puppeteer-line:miscworks.net</a> Issue page: <a href="https://src.miscworks.net/fair/matrix-puppeteer-line/issues" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">https://src.miscworks.net/fair/matrix-puppeteer-line/issues</a></p>
         </blockquote>

         <h3 id="thunderbird-matrix-support" style="position:relative"><a href="#thunderbird-matrix-support" aria-label="thunderbird matrix support permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Thunderbird Matrix support</h3>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@freaktechnik:humanoids.be" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">freaktechnik</a> announced:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p><a href="https://thunderbird.net" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Thunderbird</a> now has Matrix support based on <code class="language-text">matrix-js-sdk</code> enabled in the Nightly builds.</p>
          <p>The star feature is probably that we support multiple Matrix accounts in the same client. Right now all your unencrypted rooms with text messages should work fine. While we think we won't destroy your account's state, it's still recommended to use a testing account with it. During account setup, it will ask you for a password, even if the homeserver supports SSO. If you intend to log in through SSO, just leave the password field blank.</p>
          <p>We're not quite at the point where we support all the things you love about chatting with Matrix. Many of the missing features and polish to make communication successful are tracked in <a href="https://bugzilla.mozilla.org/show_bug.cgi?id=1712710" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">this meta bug</a>. The goal for that milestone is to enable Matrix in our Beta builds.</p>
          <p>You can get a Thunderbird Nightly build at the bottom of <a href="https://thunderbird.net/#channel" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">thunderbird.net</a> by switching from "Beta Channel" to "Nightly Channel". If you run into bugs with the Matrix integration, please report them through <a href="https://bugzilla.mozilla.org/enter_bug.cgi?product=Chat%20Core&amp;component=Matrix" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">this form</a>. When filing a bug, please include debug logs. You can copy the debug logs for the account by going to the "Show Accounts" dialog, right clicking the account and selecting "Copy Debug Log". Note that the debug log may contain information from any of your conversations, so you might want to check the contents before posting it anywhere.</p>
         </blockquote>
         <p>Also, check out Matrix Live!</p>

         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@deepbluev7:neko.dev" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Nico (@deepbluev7:neko.dev)</a> told us:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>Callum, our GSoC student, after spending some time on Synapse, had now his first go at Nheko's codebase. He implemented, that you can now just enter the server name on registration instead of the full URL. This means entering conduit.rs or matrix.org works now nicely, since those servers are actually hosted at a different URL. He's now working on the Token Registration MSC, which he will implement in Synapse and Nheko, so exciting times ahead!</p>
          <p>We also had a small contribution from pcworld, who fixed that if you only viewed the room list in the narrow layout, you would not get notifications for the last selected room.</p>
          <p>I'll leave you with some words, that you may have heard a few times already: "Watch this space for next weeks update!"</p>
         </blockquote>

         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@afranke:matrix.org" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Alexandre Franke</a> reported:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>A dozen merge requests have been integrated in our fractal-next branch since <a href="https://matrix.org/blog/2021/05/28/this-week-in-matrix-2021-05-28#fractal-updates" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">last week</a>.</p>
          <p>Amongst the more trivial changes, Julian made sure rooms are added to the sidebar in batch (<a href="https://gitlab.gnome.org/GNOME/fractal/-/merge_requests/737" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">!737</a>) to improve performances, added in-app notifications for invite errors (<a href="https://gitlab.gnome.org/GNOME/fractal/-/merge_requests/760" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">!760</a>), added a menu entry to leave rooms (<a href="https://gitlab.gnome.org/GNOME/fractal/-/merge_requests/769" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">!769</a>), and implemented display of user and room avatars (<a href="https://gitlab.gnome.org/GNOME/fractal/-/merge_requests/770" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">!770</a>). We also gained a right-click-menu entry to display event sources thanks to Kévin (<a href="https://gitlab.gnome.org/GNOME/fractal/-/merge_requests/766" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">!766</a>).</p>
         </blockquote>

           </svg></a>Element Clients</h3>
         <p>Updates provided by the teams.</p>
         <p><strong>Delight team</strong></p>
         <ul>
          <li>We’re continuing progress on implementing Blurhash on Web &amp; Android to improve the image loading experience, especially on low bandwidth</li>
          <li>On Spaces, we’ve started working on the ability to drag and drop to re-order Spaces, along with improving adding aliases to public Spaces</li>
         </ul>
         <p><strong>Web</strong></p>
         <ul>
          <li>1.7.30 RC on staging
           <ul>
            <li>Improved layout performance in the timeline and room list</li>
            <li>Refined the message action bar UI</li>
           </ul></li>
          <li>Continuing to improve application performance
           <ul>
            <li>Recent focus on minimising browser layout work when things change</li>
            <li>Reducing DOM size</li>
           </ul></li>
          <li>Working on Apple silicon desktop builds</li>
         </ul>
         <p><strong>iOS</strong></p>
         <ul>
          <li><a href="https://github.com/vector-im/element-ios/releases/tag/v1.4.0" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">1.4.0</a> is available on the public TestFlight. We expect to make it available on the App Store on Monday. It has: 
           <ul>
            <li>Performance improvements</li>
            <li>Crash fixes</li>
            <li>New languages: Esperanto, Portuguese (Brazil), Kabyle, Norwegian, Swedish, Japanese and Welsh.</li>
            <li>There are some API breaks in MatrixSDK due to those performance improvements.</li>
            <li>We have now a MXLog module with log levels! It is now possible to disable all logs from MatrixSDK</li>
           </ul></li>
          <li>We continued to work on performance and stability and will continue to for the coming sprint period: <a href="https://github.com/vector-im/element-ios/milestone/55" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">https://github.com/vector-im/element-ios/milestone/55</a> </li>
         </ul>
         <p><strong>Android</strong></p>
         <ul>
          <li>1.1.8 has been released to production, and 1.1.9 has been released to beta on the PlayStore</li>
          <li>We are currently working with the design team on the light and dark theme of the application, especially colors and text appearance. Lots of cleanup to do...</li>
         </ul>

In the meantime, I've been making good progress on reactions, which should hopefully get released early next week. Midhun has made good progress on the right panel, ironing out the last bugs.</p>

          <p>On <strong>August 21-22</strong> the annual <strong>Fr</strong>ee and <strong>O</strong>pen <strong>S</strong>ource <strong>Con</strong>ference (short <a href="https://www.froscon.de/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">FrOSCon</a>) will take place.          <h2 id="dept-of-interesting-projects-?" style="position:relative"><a href="#dept-of-interesting-projects-%EF%B8%8F" aria-label="dept of interesting projects ? permalink" class="anchor before">

            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Dept of Interesting Projects ??</h2>
         <h3 id="circles" style="position:relative"><a href="#circles" aria-label="circles permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Circles</h3>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@cvwright:matrix.org" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">cvwright</a> reported:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <ul>
           <li><p>Set up a new (virtual) EU homeserver in Frankfurt, so European folks can join the beta starting next week</p></li>
           <li><p>Use StoreKit to detect when a user is in Europe and should therefore use the EU homeserver, both for GDPR and to minimize latency</p></li>
           <li><p>Made some progress toward supporting <code class="language-text">m.video</code> messages</p></li>
           <li><p>Experimented with using the <a href="https://developer.apple.com/videos/play/wwdc2020/10652/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">new iOS photo picker</a> to better protect users' privacy Homepage: <a href="https://kombuchaprivacy.com/circles/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">https://kombuchaprivacy.com/circles/</a> Source code: <a href="https://github.com/KombuchaPrivacy/circles-ios" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">https://github.com/KombuchaPrivacy/circles-ios</a></p></li>
          </ul>
         </blockquote>
         <p>You can also <a href="https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/cvwright/circles-a-secure-social-app-for-friends-and-family?ref=4fxvne" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">support circles on Kickstarter</a>.</p>
         <h2 id="dept-of-ping-" style="position:relative"><a href="#dept-of-ping-" aria-label="dept of ping  permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Dept of Ping ?</h2>
         <p>Here we reveal, rank, and applaud the homeservers with the lowest ping, as measured by <a href="https://github.com/maubot/echo" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">pingbot</a>, a <a href="https://github.com/maubot/maubot" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">maubot</a> that you can host on your own server.</p>

        <h1 class="Article__Title-ejf3ys-0 kUhord"><a href="/blog/2021/06/01/synapse-1-35-0-released">Synapse 1.35.0 released</a></h1>
        <div class="Subline-z3aujq-0 fCCPho">
         2021-06-01<!-- --> —&nbsp;<a href="/blog/category/releases">Releases</a> —&nbsp;<!-- -->Dan Callahan
        </div>
        <div class="Article__PostContent-ejf3ys-1 dltekG">
         <p>Synapse 1.35.0 is out! This release focused on improving internals as we drive toward better memory performance during room joins, but more on that below.</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p><strong>Update:</strong> <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/releases/tag/v1.35.1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Synapse 1.35.1</a> was published on Thursday, June 3rd. It resolves a bug (<a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/issues/10109" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#10109</a>) which mistakenly listed invite-only rooms in the Spaces summary.</p>
          <p>We'd also like to call the attention of client developers to a deprecation: The unstable prefixes used during development of <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/matrix-doc/blob/master/proposals/2858-Multiple-SSO-Identity-Providers.md#unstable-prefix" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">MSC2858: Multiple SSO Identity Providers</a> will be removed from Synapse 1.38, due out in August. Please ensure your client supports the stable identifiers for this feature.</p>
         </blockquote>
         <h2 id="spaces-on-by-default" style="position:relative"><a href="#spaces-on-by-default" aria-label="spaces on by default permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Spaces: On by Default</h2>
         <p>Following the successful release of <a href="/blog/2021/05/17/synapse-1-34-0-released">Synapse 1.34</a>, the experimental Spaces flag is now enabled by default. If you had manually enabled the <code class="language-text">experimental_features: { spaces_enabled: true }</code> flag in your homeserver configuration, you may now remove it.</p>
         <h2 id="bug-squashing" style="position:relative"><a href="#bug-squashing" aria-label="bug squashing permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Bug Squashing</h2>
         <p>This release of Synapse fixes an issue which could cause federated room joins to fail when the join response exceeded a size limit which was too low (<a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/pull/10082" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#10082</a>). We've also improved what Synapse logs when it drops a connection in similar circumstances (<a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/pull/10091" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#10091</a>), which should aid diagnosis if a similar issue were to arise in the future.</p>
         <p>GitHub user thermaq contributed a fix (<a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/pull/10014" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#10014</a>) for a bug which could cause user presence state to become stale.</p>
         <p>Lastly our OpenTracing support now allows for profiling end-to-end performance on a per-user basis (<a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/pull/9978" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#9978</a>).</p>
         <h2 id="an-update-on-room-joins" style="position:relative"><a href="#an-update-on-room-joins" aria-label="an update on room joins permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>An Update on Room Joins</h2>
         <p>We've been hammering away at shrinking Synapse's memory footprint when joining large / complex rooms, and while we're not there yet, the end is in sight! In particular, this release includes many internal refactorings, including using <a href="https://pypi.org/project/ijson/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">ijson</a> to parse the JSON response to <code class="language-text">/send_join</code> (<a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/pull/9958" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#9958</a>), clearing the way for substantial improvements.</p>
         <p>Memory usage still spikes because we're effectively doing the same work with a different library, but ijson's design allows for iterative parsing. This will pay dividends once we modify the code downstream of <code class="language-text">/send_join</code> to take advantage of it.</p>
         <p>Concretely, Erik Johnston has an experimental branch of Synapse which completely eliminates the memory spike:</p>
         <p><img src="/blog/img/2021-06-01-synapse-1.35-join-memory.png" alt="Memory usage graph for Synapse 1.33, 1.35, and an experimental branch"></p>
         <p>The remaining work is centered on splitting that branch into self-contained, reviewable pull requests, like a rewrite of the Synapse Keyring class (<a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/pull/10035" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#10035</a>). After that's merged, we'll need to make one further change to properly batch up work, at which point we should attain the efficiency gains from Erik's experiment.</p>
         <h2 id="everything-else" style="position:relative"><a href="#everything-else" aria-label="everything else permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Everything Else</h2>
         <p>GitHub user savyajha contributed a security hardened systemd unit file which effectively sandboxes Synapse (<a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/pull/9803" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#9803</a>). While not enabled by default, we'd encourage security conscious users to review the <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/blob/v1.35.0/contrib/systemd/override-hardened.conf" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">example file</a> and associated <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/blob/v1.35.0/docs/systemd-with-workers/README.md#hardening" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">documentation</a>.</p>
         <p>Please see the <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/blob/v1.35.0/CHANGES.md" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Release Notes</a> for a complete list of changes in this release.</p>
         <p>Synapse is a Free and Open Source Software project, and we'd like to extend our thanks to everyone who contributed to this release, including <a href="https://github.com/dklimpel" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">dklimpel</a>, <a href="https://github.com/jerinjtitus" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">jerinjtitus</a>, <a href="https://github.com/junquera" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">junquera</a>, <a href="https://github.com/lonyeon" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">lonyeon</a>, <a href="https://github.com/savyajha" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">savyajha</a>, and <a href="https://github.com/thermaq" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">thermaq</a>.</p>
        </div>
        <div class="Article__LineBreak-ejf3ys-2 kgzjyp"></div>
       </div>
       <div class="mxcontent__main__post">
        <h1 class="Article__Title-ejf3ys-0 kUhord"><a href="/blog/2021/05/28/this-week-in-matrix-2021-05-28">This Week in Matrix 2021-05-28</a></h1>
        <div class="Subline-z3aujq-0 fCCPho">
         2021-05-28<!-- --> —&nbsp;<a href="/blog/category/this-week-in-matrix">This Week in Matrix</a> —&nbsp;<!-- -->Andrew Morgan
        </div>
        <div class="Article__PostContent-ejf3ys-1 dltekG">
         <h2 id="matrix-live-" style="position:relative"><a href="#matrix-live-" aria-label="matrix live  permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Matrix Live ?</h2>
         <div class="gatsby-resp-iframe-wrapper" style="padding-bottom:56.25%;position:relative;height:0;overflow:hidden"> <iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/4vr9RRYNWWE" title="YouTube video player" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen style="position:absolute;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%"></iframe> 
         </div>
         <br>A classic "Matthew &amp; Amandine" episode. This week: Spaces, Reputation, Low-Bandwidth, P2P &amp; more!
         <h2 id="dept-of-spec-" style="position:relative"><a href="#dept-of-spec-" aria-label="dept of spec  permalink" class="anchor before">

         <h3 id="synapse-media-proxy" style="position:relative"><a href="#synapse-media-proxy" aria-label="synapse media proxy permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>synapse-media-proxy</h3>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@f0x:pixie.town" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">f0x</a> announced:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>I've been working on a smart media worker/proxy, to offload initial spikes in traffic for homeservers behind slower network uplinks.</p>
          <p>There's a <code class="language-text">&lt;remote&gt;</code> component that sits on a small vps, handling the upload and download endpoints (and soon, thumbnails), with an in-memory cache to quickly respond to requests. Media still gets forwarded to the <code class="language-text">&lt;local&gt;</code> component where it gets stored in Synapse's media folder with an accompanying database entry, so all media is still stored long-term in the way Synapse expects it to be, so the proxy can be removed at any point. </p>
          <p>Currently not production ready but you're welcome to snoop around the repo :)</p>
          <p><a href="https://git.pixie.town/f0x/synapse-media-proxy" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">https://git.pixie.town/f0x/synapse-media-proxy</a></p>
         </blockquote>
         <p>Seems like quite a useful project! Other adventures in splitting out the media server from the homeserver include TravisR's <a href="https://github.com/turt2live/matrix-media-repo/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">matrix-media-repo project</a>.</p>

           </svg></a>libera.chat IRC network news</h3>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@Half-Shot:half-shot.uk" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Half-Shot</a> tells us:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>Hey folks, some of you (well, frankly most of you) wanted to hear about our plans for libera.chat. I've been hard at work this week building a brand new bridge which is hosted on the libera.chat homeserver and it's nearly ready to go. We're just making a few final preparations before taking it out of beta, but it's currently available as a portaling bridge. You can currently reach any channel on libera.chat by joining <code class="language-text">#&lt;channel_name&gt;:libera.chat</code>. You can also add the homeserver to your room directory in your Matrix client to search all the bridged rooms.</p>
          <p>We're also hanging out in <a href="https://matrix.to/#/#libera-matrix:libera.chat" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#libera-matrix:libera.chat</a>, if you have any questions. Of course, the bridge is proving to be very popular so please be patient :)</p>
         </blockquote>
         <p>Definitely one of the most sought-after Matrix bridges lately. Props to Half-Shot, Libera.Chat and everyone else for getting it all together in such short notice.</p>
         <h3 id="heisenbridge-updates" style="position:relative"><a href="#heisenbridge-updates" aria-label="heisenbridge updates permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Heisenbridge Updates</h3>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@hifi:vi.fi" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">hifi</a> told us:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <h4 id="plumbing-irc-channels-?" style="position:relative"><a href="#plumbing-irc-channels-%F0%9F%A7%91" aria-label="plumbing irc channels ? permalink" class="anchor before">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
             <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
            </svg></a>Plumbing IRC channels ???</h4>
          <p>Somewhat experimental feature that has landed this week is the ability to use single puppeting in a public Matrix room to bridge IRC channels.</p>
          <p>This support comes through a new <code class="language-text">PLUMB</code> admin command for network rooms that will ask the bridge bot to join a public Matrix room and an IRC channel.</p>
          <p>On IRC side there will be only a single user/bot that will relay messages from Matrix users. This is a stop-gap between fully puppeting Matrix users on IRC and doesn't need explicit permission from an IRC network to use by channel operators as long as bots are allowed.</p>
          <p>On Matrix side puppets will join and leave based on their presence on the IRC channel. The bridge bot does not need any special permissions in a room as it doesn't do permission synchronization so it can be kept without any power levels.</p>
          <p>Unplumbing a room is as simple as kicking the bridge out and it will take the puppets with it.</p>
          <p>As this is a fairly new feature it does have some rough edges so feedback is greatly appreciated.</p>
          <p>With all this said, if you're in the need to bridge any IRC channel on any network with little friction, Heisenbridge should have you covered!</p>
          <h4 id="sasl-support-" style="position:relative"><a href="#sasl-support-" aria-label="sasl support  permalink" class="anchor before">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
             <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
            </svg></a>SASL support ?</h4>
          <p>If you're using Heisenbridge to connect to Libera.Chat from a network block that has SASL enforcement enabled (like some VPS providers) you can now configure SASL credentials to authenticate at connection time to bypass this restriction.</p>
          <p>This only implements SASL PLAIN for now. Certificate authentication may be looked at in the future.</p>
          <h4 id="but-thats-not-all" style="position:relative"><a href="#but-thats-not-all" aria-label="but thats not all permalink" class="anchor before">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
             <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
            </svg></a>But that's not all</h4>
          <ul>
           <li><p>Identd will now always provide a unique ident for everyone</p></li>
           <li><p>Improved detection for stalled connections</p></li>
           <li><p>IRC user ghosting issues fixed for good ?</p></li>
           <li><p>Server TLS cert checking fixes, self-signed support</p></li>
           <li><p>Initial bridge DM invites should go through more reliably</p></li>
           <li><p><code class="language-text">QUIT</code> command to leave from all networks in one go</p></li>
           <li><p>Automatic Docker Hub images from master (amd64 and arm64)</p></li>
          </ul>
          <p>In addition Heisenbridge is now featured on <a href="https://matrix.org/bridges/#irc" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">matrix.org</a> ?</p>
         </blockquote>

           </svg></a>matrix-puppeteer-line Updates</h3>
         <p><a href="https://src.miscworks.net/fair/matrix-puppeteer-line" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">matrix-puppeteer-line</a> is a bridge for LINE Messenger based on running LINE's Chrome extension in Puppeteer.</p>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@fair:miscworks.net" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Fair</a> offered:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>This week brings a variety of assorted bugfixes &amp; feature improvements in the <code class="language-text">testing</code> branch. Included are:</p>
          <ul>
           <li><p>Support for <code class="language-text">m.sticker</code> events for LINE stickers (with an option to use <code class="language-text">m.image</code> if preferred)</p></li>
           <li><p>Clear resolution of LINE emojis, and a config option to scale them (since they're tiny by default)</p></li>
           <li><p>Less frequent re-downloading of already-seen LINE stickers/emoji (there are limits to this, but it's still an improvement)</p></li>
           <li><p>Option to disable syncing LINE stickers/emoji (in case re-hosting LINE imagery is a liability)</p></li>
           <li><p>More reliable message syncing (should never get "Decrypting message..." or invisible images/stickers/emoji anymore)</p></li>
           <li><p>Fix crashes during inbound message &amp; read receipt syncing of multi-user rooms</p></li>
          </ul>
          <p>Like last time, testing is much appreciated ?</p>
          <p>Remaining big tasks are:</p>
          <ul>
           <li><p>Rework message syncing so that receiving a message doesn't require "viewing" the LINE chat in the Puppeteer-controlled browser, which will make LINE send a read receipt even though you may not actually have read the message yourself (I mentioned this a while ago; it's still a todo)</p></li>
           <li><p>Support for multiple bridge users at once (A public instance of the bridge will only be considered once multi-user support is ready)</p></li>
          </ul>
          <p>Discussion: <a href="https://matrix.to/#/#matrix-puppeteer-line:miscworks.net" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#matrix-puppeteer-line:miscworks.net</a> </p>
          <p>Issue page: <a href="https://src.miscworks.net/fair/matrix-puppeteer-line/issues" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">https://src.miscworks.net/fair/matrix-puppeteer-line/issues</a></p>

           </svg></a>Fractal Updates</h3>
         <p><a href="https://wiki.gnome.org/Apps/Fractal" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Fractal</a> is a Matrix client written in Rust, and one of the first to use the <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/matrix-rust-sdk" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">matrix-rust-sdk</a>!</p>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@afranke:matrix.org" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Alexandre Franke</a> offered:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>Since <a href="https://matrix.org/blog/2021/05/21/this-week-in-matrix-2021-05-21#fractal" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">last week</a>, a couple things landed in <code class="language-text">fractal-next</code>. Julian added support for accepting/rejecting invites (<a href="https://gitlab.gnome.org/GNOME/fractal/-/merge_requests/754" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">!754</a>/<a href="https://gitlab.gnome.org/GNOME/fractal/-/issues/759" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#759</a>). Kévin did an <a href="https://gitlab.gnome.org/GNOME/fractal/-/merge_requests/759" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">internal restructuring of how we handle the SyncResponse in !759</a>. The visible consequence for users is that room categories (also known as tags) are updated directly in Fractal when the user changes it from an other client. He also switched from comrak to <a href="https://docs.rs/ruma/0.1.1/ruma/events/room/message/struct.TextMessageEventContent.html#method.markdown" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">ruma’s markdown</a> in <a href="https://gitlab.gnome.org/GNOME/fractal/-/merge_requests/756" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">!756</a>. It shouldn’t have any impact for users, but should mean less code in the end on our side and more consistent code as well.</p>
         </blockquote>

         <h3 id="element-client-updates" style="position:relative"><a href="#element-client-updates" aria-label="element client updates permalink" class="anchor before">

         <p>Crafted by the <a href="https://element.io" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Element</a> teams.</p>
         <p><strong>Delight</strong></p>
         <ul>
          <li>Spaces: We’ve been listening to, investigating, triaging and organising feedback from the beta so far. There’s a lot to get through, but thanks to everyone who has submitted feedback in-app in Element so far! The insight has been invaluable and is instrumental in shaping up our next milestones.</li>
          <li>Papercuts: We’re also organising and fixing small issues throughout Element, biasing for highly visible issues which have the greatest impact and reach, affectionately titled ‘papercuts’. Expect more info on these soon, but for now a fun one to highlight is we’re implementing <a href="https://github.com/woltapp/blurhash" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">blurhash</a> on Web &amp; Android (with iOS to follow soon after) to improve previewing and viewing images, especially when on low bandwidth.</li>
         </ul>
         <p><strong>Web</strong></p>
         <ul>
          <li>1.7.29 released
           <ul>
            <li>Improved startup performance by focusing decryption on recent rooms</li>
            <li>Fixed reaction duplication</li>
           </ul></li>
          <li>Sorting out why we sometimes see "<a href="https://github.com/vector-im/element-web/issues/9422#issuecomment-843366412" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">missing translations</a>" hopefully for good this time</li>
          <li>Continuing to improve application performance</li>
          <li>Started work on Apple silicon desktop builds</li>
         </ul>
         <p><strong>iOS</strong></p>
         <ul>
          <li>We continued to work on technical subjects:
           <ul>
            <li>Stabilisation and performance improvements</li>
            <li>New logging system. It will be possible to disable all logs for MatrixSDK, MatrixKit and Element-iOS</li>
            <li>The code that manages application navigation in Element-iOS has been updated. It will allow us to add a slide menu to display things like user spaces.</li>
           </ul></li>
         </ul>
         <p><strong>Android</strong></p>
         <ul>
          <li>Element Android 1.1.8 has been released on the beta track of the Google PlayStore. It will probably be pushed to production at the beginning of next week. The Android matrix SDK2 has also been released.</li>
          <li>This week, we implemented the ability to change the network when looking in the room directory. Also gitter.im has been added to the default network list. See some screenshots in <a href="https://github.com/vector-im/element-android/pull/3419" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">https://github.com/vector-im/element-android/pull/3419</a> </li>
          <li>Lots of improvements regarding Spaces have also landed to develop.</li>
          <li>Besides that, we are still fixing issues and perform regular maintenance on the project</li>
         </ul>

           </svg></a>Dept of SDKs and Frameworks ?</h2>
         <h3 id="autodiscover-server-configuration" style="position:relative"><a href="#autodiscover-server-configuration" aria-label="autodiscover server configuration permalink" class="anchor before">

           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Airlock, the space invite bot</h3>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@robintown:townsendandsmith.ml" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Robin</a> announced:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>If you want to use spaces to run an invite-only community, but can't wait for knocking and restricted room membership to make their way into a stable room version, you may be interested in <a href="https://gitlab.com/robintown/airlock" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Airlock</a>, a very simple bot that I wrote to automatically invite people to a space's rooms and subspaces when they join.</p>
          <p>It requires zero configuration—just invite the bot to your space and all of the rooms and subspaces within it, make sure it has invite permissions, and you're good to go! You're welcome to use my hosted version <a href="https://matrix.to/#/@airlock:townsendandsmith.ml" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">@airlock:townsendandsmith.ml</a>, or <a href="https://gitlab.com/robintown/airlock#running-the-bot-yourself" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">run it yourself</a>.</p>
         </blockquote>
         <p>It's great to see people building useful tools to bridge the gap as Spaces inches closer out of beta.</p>

         <h3 id="host-your-blog-on-matrix" style="position:relative"><a href="#host-your-blog-on-matrix" aria-label="host your blog on matrix permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Host your blog on Matrix</h3>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@evol:evolved.systems" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">evol</a> told us:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>About a month ago I came up with the idea that it would be interesting to use Matrix as an API for a blog. Sometime later it turned out that it's possible, and one thing led to another, and now I have a blog hosted on Matrix ?</p>
          <p>Long story short, the blog is a space and each post is a room within that space. This allows you to read the posts in your Matrix client of choice and also have discussions right underneath the content. </p>
          <p>You can read more details on how it's done on the blog itself (incl. links to ugly code on my Github): <a href="https://evolved.systems/hosting-a-blog-on-matrix/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">https://evolved.systems/hosting-a-blog-on-matrix/</a>. If you want to chat about this, join <a href="https://matrix.to/#/#blog:evolved.systems" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#blog:evolved.systems</a> !</p>
         </blockquote>
         <p>Longtime readers may remember Luke Barnard's take on the concept of Blogs built on Matrix back in 2019 with <a href="https://lukebarnard.co.uk/blog/post/journal-is-deployed/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Journal</a>. It's really exciting to see a modern version of this concept - and using Spaces no less!</p>
         <h3 id="server_stats-updates" style="position:relative"><a href="#server_stats-updates" aria-label="server_stats updates permalink" class="anchor before">

         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@mtrnord:nordgedanken.dev" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">MTRNord</a> said:</p>

         <p>Here we reveal, rank, and applaud the homeservers with the lowest ping, as measured by <a href="https://github.com/maubot/echo" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">pingbot</a>, a <a href="https://github.com/maubot/maubot" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">maubot</a> that you can host on your own server.</p>

         <h3 id="synapse" style="position:relative"><a href="#synapse" aria-label="synapse permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Synapse</h3>
         <p>Synapse is a popular homeserver written in Python.</p>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@callahad:matrix.org" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">callahad</a> offered:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>The big news this week was the launch of Spaces, supported by the release of <a href="https://matrix.org/blog/2021/05/17/synapse-1-34-0-released" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Synapse 1.34.0</a>.</p>
          <p>However, there were quite a few other fixes, improvements, and additions: I'd encourage you to read the <a href="https://matrix.org/blog/2021/05/17/synapse-1-34-0-released" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">release announcement</a> for those.</p>
          <p>But more than anything, we're hard at work realizing the room-join memory improvements we talked about in <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=694VuhmVmfo" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">last week's Matrix Live</a>, and we expect to have some exciting news to share next week. Concretely: <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/pull/9958" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">the pull request</a> to support incremental parsing of join responses was merged, and several pull requests (<a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/pull/10017" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#10017</a>, <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/pull/10018" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#10018</a>, <a href="https://github.com/matrix-org/synapse/pull/10035" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#10035</a>) to simplify and slim down the code for verifying event signatures are in review.</p>
          <p>See you next week! ?</p>
         </blockquote>
         <h3 id="conduit" style="position:relative"><a href="#conduit" aria-label="conduit permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Conduit</h3>
         <p>Conduit is a Matrix homeserver written in Rust <a href="https://conduit.rs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">https://conduit.rs</a></p>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@timokoesters:fachschaften.org" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">timokoesters</a> said:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>Here are some Conduit news!</p>
          <ul>
           <li><p>Feature: Handle incoming read receipts over federation</p></li>
           <li><p>Feature: Send read receipts over federation (MVP done)</p></li>
           <li><p>Improvement: Make UIAA (user-interactive authentication API) work like in Synapse (this gives us better client support)</p></li>
           <li><p>Refactor: Sending code refactored to make EDUs over federation possible</p></li>
           <li><p>Fix: Remove old presence events when restarting Conduit</p></li>
           <li><p>Fix: Array bounds bug in server_server.rs</p></li>
           <li><p>Fix: Power level content override adds to the default event instead of replacing it</p></li>
          </ul>
         </blockquote>
         <h2 id="homeserver-deployment-?" style="position:relative"><a href="#homeserver-deployment-%EF%B8%8F" aria-label="homeserver deployment ? permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Homeserver Deployment ??</h2>

           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Element Client Updates</h3>
         <p>Submitted by the teams</p>
         <p><strong>Delight</strong></p>
         <ul>
          <li>Spaces are now live! ? Test them on Element Web, Desktop &amp; Android (iOS is coming soon!)</li>
          <li>In short, Spaces are a new way to group rooms and people together, and are slated to replace legacy groups/communities</li>
          <li>We’d love your feedback! Either submitted in app or in <a href="https://matrix.to/#/#spaces-feedback:matrix.org" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">#spaces-feedback:matrix.org</a></li>
          <li><a href="https://element.io/blog/spaces-the-next-frontier/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Read the full blog post</a></li>
         </ul>
         <p><strong>Web</strong></p>
         <ul>
          <li>1.7.28 released
           <ul>
            <li>New spaces Beta (new way of grouping rooms and people)</li>
            <li>Added support for slash commands working in edits</li>
           </ul></li>
          <li>1.7.29-rc.1 on staging
           <ul>
            <li>Improved startup performance by focusing decryption on recent rooms</li>
            <li>Fixed reaction duplication</li>
           </ul></li>
          <li>Continuing to pursue application performance generally</li>
          <li>Improving day to day developer experience with more TypeScript conversion</li>
         </ul>
         <p><strong>iOS</strong></p>
         <ul>
          <li><a href="https://github.com/vector-im/element-ios/releases/tag/v1.3.9" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">1.3.9</a> has been published on the app store </li>
          <li>Some performance improvements have been merged on develop:
           <ul>
            <li>Reduce the number of decryptions. A decryption takes about 5ms on iPhone X. On an account with 500 rooms this allows us to skip thousands of decryptions on an initial sync</li>
            <li>Those decryptions do not happen anymore on the main thread</li>
           </ul></li>
         </ul>
         <p><strong>Android</strong></p>
         <ul>
          <li>Lots of dependency upgrade following the release with Space (1.1.7).</li>
          <li>Next release candidate, 1.1.8 will also contain improvements on Spaces.</li>
          <li>We have set up towncrier flow to better handle changelog generation.</li>
          <li>Also Element Android project is now using GitHub actions, but it cannot run the integration tests for the moment.</li>
         </ul>
         <h3 id="fractal" style="position:relative"><a href="#fractal" aria-label="fractal permalink" class="anchor before">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Fractal</h3>
         <p><a href="https://matrix.to/#/@afranke:matrix.org" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Alexandre Franke</a> offered:</p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>As announced in <a href="https://matrix.org/blog/2021/05/20/google-summer-of-code-2021#fractal" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">the general Matrix GSoC post</a>, we are lucky to get two interns this year again. Alejandro (whose previous work includes <a href="https://gitlab.gnome.org/GNOME/fractal/-/merge_requests/626" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">switching to matrix-rust-sdk for syncs</a>) will implement multi-account support, while Kai (also <a href="https://gitlab.gnome.org/GNOME/fractal/-/merge_requests?scope=all&amp;utf8=%E2%9C%93&amp;state=merged&amp;author_username=V02460" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">a regular contributor</a> by now) will help bring our application rewrite to the same functionality level as our current nightly and stable versions. Both projects will build on top of Fractal Next.</p>
          <p>Julian came back from his vacation and immediately got quite busy reviewing and merging contributions from others. Kevin (also known as zecakeh) and him made good progress on several fronts:</p>
          <ul>
           <li><p>Room handling was improved. We now keep track of whether the user joined them, left them, or has been invited to them, as well as their categories (favourites, low priority…).</p></li>
           <li><p>The sidebar uses these categories and now uses a single list with <a href="https://gtk-rs.org/gtk4-rs/git/docs/gtk4/struct.FilterListModel.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">GtkFilterListModels</a> instead of one list per category. The greatly simplifies code for things like moving a room from one category to another.</p></li>
           <li><p>History style has been tweaked, state events and timestamps have been added.</p></li>
           <li><p>Markdown can be enabled from the newly implemented popover and the message composer offers syntax highlighting, although a bug currently makes it so that sent messages are still not sent with a <code class="language-text">formatted_body</code>.</p></li>
           <li><p>A persistent state store is used to load rooms on startup while sync is in progress.</p></li>
          </ul>
          <p>Last but not least, new contributor Raatty implemented <a href="https://gitlab.gnome.org/GNOME/fractal/-/merge_requests/735" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">room name and topic display in the header bar</a>.</p>
         </blockquote>

         <h2 id="dept-of-sdks-and-frameworks-?" style="position:relative"><a href="#dept-of-sdks-and-frameworks-%F0%9F%A7%B0" aria-label="dept of sdks and frameworks ? permalink" class="anchor before">
